
-----title
湖州 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='04733226d6334fecb09574a1cb3a1052_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("04733226d6334fecb09574a1cb3a1052");'><span id='04733226d6334fecb09574a1cb3a1052_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=774')">772-774年</a>，1-3岁</div><div id='04733226d6334fecb09574a1cb3a1052' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=772&endYear=772')">772年</a>　是年生于乌程县署。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=773&endYear=773')">773年</a>　乳病暴作，改名绅。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=774&endYear=774')">774年</a>　是年或居乌程，姑系于此。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='767ccaf74a6d4b69901efd1cc1b989a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("767ccaf74a6d4b69901efd1cc1b989a2");'><span id='767ccaf74a6d4b69901efd1cc1b989a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=791')">790-791年</a>，19-20岁</div><div id='767ccaf74a6d4b69901efd1cc1b989a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=790&endYear=790')">790年</a>　客游乌程。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=791&endYear=791')">791年</a>　再游乌程。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
无锡

id='poem_sentence_7_27057'>杨柳长庭柯，兰荃覆阶草。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27057'>旌旄光里舍，骑服欢妻嫂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27013'>俱是海天黄叶信，两逢霜节菊花秋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27013'>望中白鹤怜归翼，行处青苔恨昔游。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27013'>还向窗间<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作竹窗）</span>名姓下，数行添记别离愁<span class='inlineComment2'>（万首绝句分为二首）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27013_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27013'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27013_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26987' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26987?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别石泉</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26987")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26987_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_26987'>在惠山寺松竹之下，甘爽，乃人间灵液，清澄鉴肌骨（清澄见肌骨），含漱开神虑，茶得此水，皆尽芳味。</div><div id='poem_preface_26987_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26987'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26987'>素沙见底空无色，青石潜流暗有声。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26987'>微渡竹风涵淅沥，细浮松月透轻明。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26987'>桂凝秋露添灵液，茗折香芽泛<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_26987", 26987, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>玉英</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26987'>应是梵宫连洞府，浴池今化醒泉清。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26987'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26987_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26986' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26986' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26986?labeling=true' target='_blank'>别双温树</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26986")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26986_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_26986'>往年于惠山书房前手植，今已乔柯，数寻干云，葱翠荫日。此树移过江多死，有类丹橘。</div><div id='poem_preface_26986_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26986'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26986'>翠条盈尺怜孤秀，植向西窗待月轩。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26986'>轻剪绿丝秋叶暗，密扶纤干夏阴繁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26986'>故山手种<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作植）</span>空<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_26986", 26986, "Clauses/4/Comments/1")'>怀想</span>，温室心知不敢言。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26986'>看尔拂云今得地，莫随陵谷改深根。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26986_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26986'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26986_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=799&endYear=799')">799年</a>　是年或居常州无锡，姑系于此。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='dce570efed6a4435a3ff2e150f817bd0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("dce570efed6a4435a3ff2e150f817bd0");'><span id='dce570efed6a4435a3ff2e150f817bd0_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　返回无锡县寓居。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='d0dec0f4360047de9b259bfe24907d7e_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　是年作诗，姑系于此。作品：《过梅里七首家于无锡四十载今敝庐数堵犹存今列题于后》<div id='poem_26984' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26984' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26984?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过梅里七首　家于无锡四十载今敝庐数堵犹存今列题于后<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>忆题惠山寺书堂</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26984")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26984_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26984'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26984'>故山一别光阴改，秋露清风岁月多。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26984'>松下壮心年少去，池边衰影老人过。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26984'>白云生灭依岩岫，青桂荣枯托薜萝。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26984'>惟有此身长是客，又驱旌旆寄烟波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26984_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26984'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26984_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26983' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26983' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26983?labeling=true' target='_blank'>过梅里七首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其七 </span>家于无锡四十载今敝庐数堵犹存今列题于后</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26983")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26983_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_26983'>顷年无锡閒居，里人献鹤雏，余驯养之。周岁，羽毛既成，见其宛颈长鸣，有烟霄之志。开笼放之，一举冲天，复回翔久之，乃去。</div><div id='poem_preface_26983_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26983'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26983'>羽毛似雪无瑕点，顾影秋池舞白云。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26983'>闲整素仪三岛近，回飘清唳九霄闻。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26983'>好风<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_26983", 26983, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>顺举</span>应摩日，逸翮将成<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作翔）</span>莫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_26983", 26983, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>恋群</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26983'>凌励坐看空碧外，更怜凫鹭老江濆。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26983_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26983'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26983_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27056' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27056' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27056_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27056'>余顷居梅里，常于惠山肆业。旧室犹在，垂白重游，追感多思，因效吴均体。</div><div id='poem_preface_27056_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27056'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27056'>上家山，家山依旧好。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27056'>昔去松桂长，今来容须老。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27056'>上家山，临古道。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27056'>高低入云树，芜没连天草。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27056'>草色绿萋萋，寒蛩遍草啼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27056'>噪鸦啼树远，行雁帖云齐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27056'>岩光翻落日，僧火开经室。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27056'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27056", 27056, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>竹洞</span>磬声长，松楼钟韵疾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27056'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_27056", 27056, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>苔阶</span>泉溜鈌，石甃青莎密。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27056'>旧径行处迷，前交坐中失。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27056'>叹息整华冠，持杯强自欢。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27056'>笑歌怜稚孺，弦竹纵吹弹。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27056'>山明溪月上，酒满心聊放。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27056'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_27056", 27056, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>丱发</span>此淹留，垂丝匪闲旷。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27056'>青山不可上，昔事还惆怅。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27056_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27056'>况复白头人，追怀空望望。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27057'>衰禽识<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作息）</span>旧木，疲马知归道。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27057_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27060?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其六 </span>翡翠坞</a><span class='authorDate'>（798年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27060'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27060'>翡翠飞飞绕莲坞，一啄嘉鱼一鸣舞。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27060'>莲茎触散莲叶欹，露滴珠光似还浦。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27060'>虞人掠水轻浮弋，翡翠惊飞飞不息。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27060'>直上层空翠影高，还向云间双比翼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27060'>弹射莫及弋不得，日暮虞人空叹息。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27060_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27060'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_27060_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9b12e1f25d224809ab6c93b4523cc7b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9b12e1f25d224809ab6c93b4523cc7b5");'><span id='9b12e1f25d224809ab6c93b4523cc7b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>，64岁</div><div id='9b12e1f25d224809ab6c93b4523cc7b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　赴任洛阳途中，至无锡，有诗。作品：《却望无锡芙蓉湖》<div id='poem_26947' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26947' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26947")'>李绅</a></span><br -----title
苏州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='355a87eb425c4881a6f4e6b1f3f9079e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("355a87eb425c4881a6f4e6b1f3f9079e");'><span id='355a87eb425c4881a6f4e6b1f3f9079e_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=794&endYear=794')">794年</a>　客游苏州，以诗受知于苏州刺史韦夏卿。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='409e7b0f74614e3e95500c267b86bb1d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("409e7b0f74614e3e95500c267b86bb1d");'><span id='409e7b0f74614e3e95500c267b86bb1d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年</a>，32岁</div><div id='409e7b0f74614e3e95500c267b86bb1d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=803&endYear=803')">803年7月</a>　客游苏州，有文。作品：《苏州画龙记》<div id='poem_1373683' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373683' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373683?labeling=true' target='_blank'>苏州画龙记</a><span class='authorDate'>（803年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373683")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373683_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373683'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373683'>自造父刘累殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373683_comment'></div>豢氏不副。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373683_comment'></div>龙不复扰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373683_comment'></div>隐去莫狎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373683_comment'></div>往时见史必书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373683_comment'></div>志代以目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373683_comment'></div>识者寡之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373683_comment'></div>故工得以诡乱形状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373683_comment'></div>神其变化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373683_comment'></div>彪炳五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373683_comment'></div>逾远真像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373683_comment'></div>盖上飞于天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373683_comment'></div>晦隔层云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373683_comment'></div>下归于泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373683_comment'></div>深入无底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373683_comment'></div>考之丹青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373683_comment'></div>难以徵验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373683_comment'></div>好事者张其画以示群目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373683_comment'></div>观者或骇疑得其状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373683_comment'></div>长洲令厅北庑有画蛟龙六焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373683_comment'></div>元素异鳞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373683_comment'></div>状殊质怪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373683_comment'></div>骧首拖尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373683_comment'></div>似随风雷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373683_comment'></div>乘栌薄楣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373683_comment'></div>若轶云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373683_comment'></div>燕雀惧栖其上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373683_comment'></div>蝼蚁罔缘其侧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1373683_comment'></div>目视光射。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1373683_comment'></div>莹无流尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1373683_comment'></div>伸盘逶迤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1373683_comment'></div>如护榱栋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1373683_comment'></div>每飞雨度牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1373683_comment'></div>疏云殷空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1373683_comment'></div>鳞鲜耀阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1373683_comment'></div>顾壁疑拔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1373683_comment'></div>志其侧曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1373683_comment'></div>僧繇弗兴之旧度模之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1373683_comment'></div>不知何人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1373683_comment'></div>二工图龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1373683_comment'></div>天与幽思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1373683_comment'></div>今是壁指远异代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1373683_comment'></div>继之图法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1373683_comment'></div>无谢于二子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1373683_comment'></div>而名漏不传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1373683_comment'></div>询于耆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1373683_comment'></div>亦绝传记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1373683_comment'></div>茂宰博陵崔君据始命余述举丹素实验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1373683_comment'></div>附邑书末简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1373683_comment'></div>庶乎后数百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1373683_comment'></div>栋宇斯变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1373683_comment'></div>龙亡其像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1373683_comment'></div>而事刻编简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1373683_comment'></div>繇昭昭然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1373683_comment'></div>时贞元癸未岁秋七月记。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1373683_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ce5474d7193440f8994ea3fa032c240f_label'><a ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　过吴门，作诗，姑系于此。作品：《过吴门二十四韵》<div id='poem_27048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27048")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27048'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27048'>烟水吴都郭，阊门架碧流。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27048'>绿杨深浅巷，青翰往来舟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27048'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27048", 27048, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>朱户</span>千家室，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27048", 27048, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>丹楹</span>百处楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27048'>水光摇极浦，草色辨长洲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27048'>忆作<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作昨）</span>麻衣翠<span id='poem_sentence_7_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27048'>桥转攒虹饮<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作影）</span>，波通斗鹢浮。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27048'>旧风犹越鼓，馀俗尚吴钩。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27048'>故馆曾闲访，遗基<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作踪）</span>亦<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_27048", 27048, "Clauses/25/Comments/1")'>遍搜</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27048'>吹台山木尽，香径佛宫秋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27048'>帐殿菰蒲掩，云房露雾收。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27048'>苧萝妖覆<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作废）</span>灭，荆棘鬼包羞。<div id='poem_sentence_15_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_27048'>风月俄黄绶，经过半白头<sup class='reference id='poem_sentence_17_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_27048'>候火分<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_27048", 27048, id='poem_sentence_18_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_27048'>水风摇䌽旆，堤柳引鸣驺。<div id='poem_sentence_19_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_27048'>问吏儿孙隔，呼名礼敬修。<div id='poem_sentence_20_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_27048'>顾瞻殊宿昔，语默过悲忧。<div id='poem_sentence_21_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_27048'>义感心空在，容衰日易偷。<div id='poem_sentence_22_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_27048'>还持沧海诏，从此布皇猷。<div id='poem_sentence_23_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_27048'></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_27048_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_27048'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_27048_0'>⑴ 贞元中，余以布衣多游吴郡中，韦夏卿首为知遇，常陪宴席段平仲、李季何、刘从周、綦毋咸十馀辈，日同杯酒。及余以太和七年领镇会稽，则当时宾客、群吏、乐徒、寺僧、里客，无一人存者，至于韦公子，凋丧略尽</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_16_27048_0'>⑵ 元和七年，余以校书郎从役，再至苏州。时范十五传正为郡，而贞元中宾客散落，半已殂谢。及宴，而伶人酒徒悉往日者，问僧，惟令起二人，已疾</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_27048_0'>⑶ 太和七年，余镇会稽，刘禹锡为郡，则元和中苏州相识，知与不知，索然皆尽。河柳衰谢，邑居更易，乃甚令威之叹也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_27048_comment'></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_27048'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(27048)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　赴镇浙东，途经苏州与刘禹锡相会。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年12月</a>　抵越州，筑杜鹃楼，为四望亭作记。作品：《四望亭记》<div id='poem_1373682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四望亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373682")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373682'>濠城之西北隅。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1373682", 1373682, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>爽耸</span>四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373682_comment'></div>纵目周视。回环者可数百里而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373682_comment'></div>尽彼目力。四封不阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373682_comment'></div>尝为废墉。无所伫望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373682_comment'></div>郡守彭城刘君字嗣之理郡之二载。步履所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373682_comment'></div>悦而创亭焉。丰约广袤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373682_comment'></div>称其所便。栋干<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1373682", 1373682, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>梯陛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373682_comment'></div>依墉以成。崇不危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373682_comment'></div>丽不侈。可以列宾筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373682_comment'></div>可以施管磬。云山左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373682_comment'></div>长淮萦带。下绕清濠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373682_comment'></div>旁阚城邑。四封五通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373682_comment'></div>皆可洞然。太和七年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373682_comment'></div>绅分命东洛。路出于濠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373682_comment'></div>始登斯亭。周目四瞩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373682_comment'></div>美乎哉。春台视和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373682_comment'></div>夏日居高明。秋以阅农功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373682_comment'></div>冬以观肃成。盖君子布和求瘼之诚志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373682_comment'></div>岂徒纵目于白雪。望云于黄鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373682_comment'></div>庾楼夕月。岘首春风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373682_comment'></div>盖一时之胜爽。无四者之眺临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373682_comment'></div>斯亭之佳景。固难俦俪哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373682_comment'></div>淮柳初变。濠泉始清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373682_comment'></div>山凝远岚。霞散馀绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373682_comment'></div>顾余尝为玉堂词臣。笔砚犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373682_comment'></div>请书亭表事。刻石记言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373682_comment'></div>癸丑岁建卯月七日。赵郡李绅书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373682_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1373682_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年12月</a>　抵越州，筑杜鹃楼，有碑铭。作品：《墨诏持经大德神异碑铭》<div id='poem_1373685' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373685' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373685?labeling=true' target='_blank'>墨诏持经大德神异碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373685")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373685_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373685'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373685'>贤劫千佛。生于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373685_comment'></div>法轮<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1373685", 1373685, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>递转</span>。应现随相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373685_comment'></div>或国王大臣。宰官居士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373685_comment'></div>降生有地。不以色相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373685_comment'></div>故如来言。以色见我。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373685_comment'></div>以音声求我。为行邪道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373685_comment'></div>不以金色瑞相。莲花化生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373685_comment'></div>降胎示报。以潜灵圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373685_comment'></div>上人姓唐氏。生于邑之安吉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373685_comment'></div>母梅氏。奇孕而梦协灵祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373685_comment'></div>在娠而不茹荤血。既生能言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373685_comment'></div>不为戏弄。未龀之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373685_comment'></div>思求佛乘。发念法华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373685_comment'></div>三月通贯。传梵音于性禀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373685_comment'></div>精护念于神契。经声一发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373685_comment'></div>而顽鄙革心。昼集夜持。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373685_comment'></div>而七部圆满。音声从容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373685_comment'></div>指顾闲雅。虽捷口利辩者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373685_comment'></div>皆随慕念。及登戒之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373685_comment'></div>僧仪首冠。西游长安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373685_comment'></div>祥风达于函关。瑞相通于帝梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373685_comment'></div>上人以持经为国。诣阙请见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373685_comment'></div>肃宗皇帝召对禁中。上拱而叹曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373685_comment'></div>昔梦吴僧。口念大乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373685_comment'></div>五光随发。音容宛若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373685_comment'></div>协我嘉徵。因赐名曰大光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373685_comment'></div>以瑞唐姓。肃宗元年降诞之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373685_comment'></div>会斋于定国寺。因赐上人墨诏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1373685_comment'></div>许以天下名寺持意往者住持。令内臣赵思温送于千佛寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1373685_comment'></div>持经道场。经四七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1373685_comment'></div>而吴音清亮。常达圣听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1373685_comment'></div>上异其事。令高力士以宣谕焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1373685_comment'></div>后居蓝田精舍。先期而寺僧梦天童来降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1373685_comment'></div>称曰。大光经声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1373685_comment'></div>达于峰顶。师既晏坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1373685_comment'></div>自见神手从天而降。拊光之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1373685_comment'></div>师乃忆先达抱玉大师。常志师言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1373685_comment'></div>令高法音。当有神辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1373685_comment'></div>夕梦神僧乳见于心。命光口饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1373685_comment'></div>自是功力显扬。神形不劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1373685_comment'></div>寻山探幽。偶坠穷谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1373685_comment'></div>龙泉莫测。沦溺其间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1373685_comment'></div>心灵了然。无所惑乱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1373685_comment'></div>因以本经多宝塔为诚。愿持十万遍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1373685_comment'></div>恍然出泉。若有神捧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1373685_comment'></div>后诏住资圣寺。大师以慈亲在吴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1373685_comment'></div>未答慈力。表乞归养。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1373685_comment'></div>恩未许还。犹系烦恼之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1373685_comment'></div>遂生无妄之疾。策蹇强力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1373685_comment'></div>将投于泉。驴伏不前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1373685_comment'></div>群乌拂顶。心既时觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1373685_comment'></div>疾乃遂瘳。昔如来双鹊巢顶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1373685_comment'></div>而定慧坚明。大师群乌摩首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1373685_comment'></div>而烦疑解脱。乃以宝轴加饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1373685_comment'></div>首戴法华。于千福寺行道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1373685_comment'></div>日夜候命。有诏许还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1373685_comment'></div>遂止乌程。崇修宝塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1373685_comment'></div>日持法华偈。以成往愿焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1373685_comment'></div>永泰元年。浙西廉察使韦元辅表大师为六郡别驾道场将念之首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1373685_comment'></div>大历癸丑岁。文忠公颜真卿领郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1373685_comment'></div>余先人主邑乌程。余生未期岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1373685_comment'></div>乳病暴作。不啼不览者七辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1373685_comment'></div>师至。命乳母洗涤焚香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1373685_comment'></div>乃朗念法华。至功德品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1373685_comment'></div>遂起席而坐。拱而开目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1373685_comment'></div>师饮以杯水。遂命乳哺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1373685_comment'></div>疾乃随愈。大师视而笑曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1373685_comment'></div>汝何愿返之速乎。因以法师易余幼名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1373685_comment'></div>贞元中。余甫弱冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1373685_comment'></div>再游霅上。舟泊之次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1373685_comment'></div>大师伫于溪侧而笑。戏拊如儿童焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1373685_comment'></div>余为州将饮醉于馆。大师引宿于道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1373685_comment'></div>夜分将醒。白光满室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1373685_comment'></div>朗然如昼。睹大师晏坐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1373685_comment'></div>妙音方阐。若开毫相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1373685_comment'></div>经音既息。光亦随敛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1373685_comment'></div>余是年西迈。辞大师于法筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1373685_comment'></div>抚余顶曰。尔得径山之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1373685_comment'></div>我则无以为谕。行矣自爱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1373685_comment'></div>去留有时。空王教平等者护念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1373685_comment'></div>大师于永贞元年十二月黑月既夕。示灭于法华寺之经院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1373685_comment'></div>兽号鸟坠。山木惊振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1373685_comment'></div>异香飘馥。三日不息。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1373685_comment'></div>是日告刺史颜防善曰。去矣人世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1373685_comment'></div>无牵梦泡。大师熙和畅达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1373685_comment'></div>无入不得。随机见教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1373685_comment'></div>经行无阂。维摩诘之俦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1373685_comment'></div>知机洞如。藏往察来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1373685_comment'></div>默而不显。晋宝公之伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1373685_comment'></div>经通梵界。瑞降天童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1373685_comment'></div>灵相神光。照融显见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1373685_comment'></div>昙上人之徒也。大哉明德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1373685_comment'></div>慈悲护世。通异相于王宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1373685_comment'></div>示法轮之宝重。昏外识于黎庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1373685_comment'></div>惧色相之迷妄。是以居若长桥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1373685_comment'></div>动如浮云。随鸥自亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1373685_comment'></div>入兽不乱。一衲四十岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1373685_comment'></div>无浣濯而居常香馥。一饭七十载。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1373685_comment'></div>资禅悦而肤体温然。余遭大师留驻于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1373685_comment'></div>而不睹大师寂灭之日。年逾耳顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1373685_comment'></div>昏寄尘劳。无法舸以济河。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1373685_comment'></div>悲火宅之迷室。忝门徒者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1373685_comment'></div>追书梵宫。时予乌台旧僚天官郎敬君守郡吴兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1373685_comment'></div>寄言刊石。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1373685_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_104_1373685'>多宝如来。闻经诵塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1373685_comment'></div>牟尼阐教。以宏正法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1373685_comment'></div>受持三世。以成贤劫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1373685_comment'></div>或降忉利。或生人天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1373685_comment'></div>金相不显。真如默传。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1373685_comment'></div>明灯继燄。水月分圆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1373685_comment'></div>示抱全德。资于上贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1373685_comment'></div>体实戒珠。心惟法镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1373685_comment'></div>怀宝不迷。含光不竞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1373685_comment'></div>希夷要妙。法凝清净。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1373685_comment'></div>发谕开蒙。藏机匿圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1373685_comment'></div>瑞协皇梦。功致天童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1373685_comment'></div>声宣梵界。响达宸聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1373685_comment'></div>降灵神手。捧溺龙宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1373685_comment'></div>迹隐三昧。心符六通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1373685_comment'></div>金粟分身。普贤驰象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1373685_comment'></div>譬喻言辞。光明显相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1373685_comment'></div>仁滋一雨。功归无量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1373685_comment'></div>法性天高。慈门海旷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1373685_comment'></div>我昔婴儿。迷蒙疾痼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1373685_comment'></div>靡日沉魄。返年师驻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1373685_comment'></div>梵音耳听。神光目睹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1373685_comment'></div>白马先镳。迷津莫溯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1373685_comment'></div>鼓音已息。慈云不浮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1373685_comment'></div>宝树摧华。祥泉涸流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1373685_comment'></div>稠林丧斧。苦海沉舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1373685_comment'></div>色相归空。法身无际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1373685_comment'></div>莫测往来。谁分显晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1373685_comment'></div>三表阐仁。深乎晏谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1373685_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_133_1373685_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8872715084334585bcbaf69cbb17f1cd_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8872715084334585bcbaf69cbb17f1cd");'><span id='8872715084334585bcbaf69cbb17f1cd_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=816&endYear=816')">816年7月</a>　在国子助教任，葬兄于长安白鹿原。作品：《唐故试太常寺奉礼郎赵郡李府君墓志文》<br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/1373676?labeling=true' target='_blank'>授韩宏河中节度使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（820年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1373676'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373676'>门下。王者统驭万宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373676_comment'></div>缉熙庶政。必有文武全器。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373676_comment'></div>柱石之臣。出壮藩岳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373676_comment'></div>入和台鼎。使其效彰中外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373676_comment'></div>声播华夷。所居而人心自宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373676_comment'></div>所莅而军令自肃。克是任者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373676_comment'></div>其惟至公。开府仪同三司守司徒兼中书令上柱国许国公食邑三千户韩宏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373676_comment'></div>受天地凝粹之气。得山川崇深之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373676_comment'></div>厚其体而庄其容。虚其心而宏其量。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373676_comment'></div>早洞戎韬之略。久膺节制之权。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373676_comment'></div>隐然大梁。克有成绩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373676_comment'></div>及功宣荡寇。志展勤王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373676_comment'></div>恳申恋阙之诚。竟遂来朝之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373676_comment'></div>位高百辟。荣冠一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373676_comment'></div>恩极而愈恭。名光而益励。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373676_comment'></div>朕方欲树以垣翰。仗乎忠贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373676_comment'></div>乃眷关河之首。实惟股肱之郡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373676_comment'></div>自昔重寄。无非元勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373676_comment'></div>是用命以上公。复兹雄镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373676_comment'></div>于戏。顷居东夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373676_comment'></div>父子偕分阃之荣。今处近郊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373676_comment'></div>伯仲并登坛之贵。道苟积于忠实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373676_comment'></div>顾何爱于宠章。往惟钦哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373676_comment'></div>副我明命。可守司徒兼中书令河中尹充河中晋绛慈隰等州节度观察处置等使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373676_comment'></div>散官勋封如故。主者施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373676_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1373676_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a -----title
天台

-----title
镇江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='fb99682cada44357ad2cee17693ac02d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("fb99682cada44357ad2cee17693ac02d");'><span id='fb99682cada44357ad2cee17693ac02d_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=806&endYear=806')">806年</a>　归觐途经润州，为浙西节度使李锜留为掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　入幕浙西，为李锜掌书记。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年9月</a>　在浙西幕，李锜叛乱，李绅不从，被执，后因锜败而得免。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=807&endYear=807')">807年</a>　在浙西幕，浙西节度使李元素欲将李绅抗锜事表于朝廷，李绅再三推让，游鹤林寺。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='c1830263e8fb4447bd0348c1b40feb94_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c1830263e8fb4447bd0348c1b40feb94");'><span id='c1830263e8fb4447bd0348c1b40feb94_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>，64岁</div><div id='c1830263e8fb4447bd0348c1b40feb94' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　赴任洛阳途中，至镇江鹤林寺，有诗。作品：《望鹤林寺》<div id='poem_27020' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27020' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27020?labeling=true' target='_blank'>望鹤林寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27020")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27020_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27020'>仍岁往来牵迫，皆不得往。元和初，在故度支尚书兄宾府，多因閒暇，经游此寺。寺内有木兰、杜鹃繁茂，人言至今犹未衰歇。</div><div id='poem_preface_27020_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27020'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27020'>鹤栖峰下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27020", 27020, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>青莲宇</span>，花发江城世界春。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27020'>红照日高殷夺火，紫凝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27020", 27020, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>霞曙</span>莹销尘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27020'>每思载酒悲前事，欲问题诗想旧身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27020'>自叹秋风劳物役，白头拘束一闲人。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27020_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27020'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27020_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
绍兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8a525e2207734dcfb136282349cfcd8e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8a525e2207734dcfb136282349cfcd8e");'><span id='8a525e2207734dcfb136282349cfcd8e_link' 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>应浙东观察使薛苹之邀客游越州并与僧人修真晤，时修真已病。作品：《龙宫寺诗并序》<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在浙东曾与薛平、冯定、灵彻唱和，唱和诗篇今已不传。<br /></div><div class='label1' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27073'>殿涌全身塔，池开<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27073", 27073, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>半月泉</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27073'>十峰排碧落，双涧合清涟<span class='inlineComment2'>（寺前后有十峰回绕，双涧合流之）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27073'>戒珠高腊护，心印祖僧传<span class='inlineComment2'>（此寺僧律严肃，持经皆承师教）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27073_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_note_27073_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=834&endYear=834')">834年10月</a>　在浙东任，祭禹庙，有诗。作品：《登（一作祭）禹庙回降雪五言二十韵》<div id='poem_27051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>登<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作祭）</span>禹庙回降雪五言二十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（834年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27051")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27051_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27051'>此诗一首，在越所作，今编入卷内。大和八年十月，冬暄无雪，自访禹庙所祷（自访禹庙祈祷）。其日回舟至湖半，阴云四合，飞霰大降者三日。积雪盈尺，浙江中流，乃分阴雪，杭州并无所沾。</div><div id='poem_preface_27051_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_sentence_3_26981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26981'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26981_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年4月</a>　在浙东任，修龙宫寺，有碑记。作品：《龙宫寺碑》<div id='poem_1373684' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373684' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373684?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龙宫寺碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373684")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373684_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373684'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373684'>会稽地滨沧海。西控长江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373684_comment'></div>自大禹疏凿了溪。人方宅土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373684_comment'></div>而南岩海迹。高下犹存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373684_comment'></div>则司其水旱。洪为云雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373684_comment'></div>乃神龙之乡。为福之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373684_comment'></div>寺曰龙宫。在剡之界灵芝乡嵊亭里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373684_comment'></div>地形爽垲。林岭依抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373684_comment'></div>刹宇颓毁。积有年所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373684_comment'></div>自创置基。三徙而安此地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373684_comment'></div>像仪消化。钟磬不扬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373684_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1373684", 1373684, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>堵波</span>已倾。法轮莫转。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373684_comment'></div>老释修真。持诫兹寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373684_comment'></div>护念常启。愿兴伽蓝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373684_comment'></div>而岁月屡迁。物力无及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373684_comment'></div>贞元十八年。余以进士客于江浙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373684_comment'></div>时适天台。与修真会于剡之阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373684_comment'></div>师言老禅有念。今兹果矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373684_comment'></div>后当领镇此道。幸愿建龙宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373684_comment'></div>以资福履。余以为孟浪之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373684_comment'></div>笑而不荅。师曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373684_comment'></div>星岁有期。愚有冥告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373684_comment'></div>暨元和三年。余罢金陵从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373684_comment'></div>河东薛公平招游镜中。师已卧病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373684_comment'></div>而约言无易。太和癸丑岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373684_comment'></div>余自分命洛阳承诏。以检校左骑省廉察于兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373684_comment'></div>岁逾再纪。而修真已为异物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373684_comment'></div>龙宫栋宇将尽。命告坟塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373684_comment'></div>因追昔言。遂以头陀僧会真部领工人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1373684_comment'></div>将以蒇事。余以俸钱三百贯□□监军使毛公承泰亦施焉以月俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1373684_comment'></div>俾从事僚吏。咸同胜因。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1373684_comment'></div>闾里慕仁。风靡争施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1373684_comment'></div>子来之功力云集。清凉之莲宇郁兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1373684_comment'></div>浃旬而垣墉四周。逾月而栋干连合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1373684_comment'></div>焕矣真界。昭乎化城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1373684_comment'></div>择静行僧居之。以总寺事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1373684_comment'></div>因具香馔。告诚法王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1373684_comment'></div>上以资我后无疆之祚。次以资神龙水府之福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1373684_comment'></div>以名寺之功力。为祐灵之显报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1373684_comment'></div>一雨之施。润洽必同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1373684_comment'></div>佛言龙王心力所致。七郡山泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1373684_comment'></div>城邑万人。介福所安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1373684_comment'></div>翳我龙德。是用回此法力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1373684_comment'></div>永资泉宫。僧斋护念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1373684_comment'></div>常为仰荅。余固不敢以修真之言自伐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1373684_comment'></div>俾竭诚以为人。刻石记言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1373684_comment'></div>于寺之刹。铭曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1373684_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_46_1373684'>沧海之隅。会稽巨泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1373684_comment'></div>惟禹功力。生人始藉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1373684_comment'></div>土壤山㠗。滨海之东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1373684_comment'></div>溟涨空阔。邈秘龙宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1373684_comment'></div>贝阙难知。珠宫莫测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1373684_comment'></div>云雨交昏。深沉不隔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1373684_comment'></div>闻法必听。依佛必降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1373684_comment'></div>岂腾溟海。亦化长江。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1373684_comment'></div>既资胜因。为龙景福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1373684_comment'></div>节宣风雨。以成播育。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1373684_comment'></div>撞钟以告。三界必闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1373684_comment'></div>惟尔龙室。昭昭不昏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1373684_comment'></div>我昔麻衣。有僧传言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1373684_comment'></div>斯人已亡。斯言不泯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1373684_comment'></div>敬报前志。以垂后功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1373684_comment'></div>建饰仪相。昭明有融。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1373684_comment'></div>普利群生。罔资已力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1373684_comment'></div>琢磨记言。垂示无斁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1373684_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1373684_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　在浙东任。作品：《龟山寺鱼池》<div id='poem_26952' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26952' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26952?labeling=true' target='_blank'>龟山寺鱼池<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26952")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_26952_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26952'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26952'>汲水添池活白莲，十千鬐鬣尽<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_26952", 26952, id='poem_sentence_2_26952'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26952_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26953' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26953' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_sentence_2_26953'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26953_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年5月</a>　除太子宾客分司东洛。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年7月</a>　离越州，越人不忍其离去，绅有诗记此事。作品：《宿越州天王寺》<div id='poem_27019' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27019' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27019?labeling=true' target='_blank'>宿越州天王寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27019'>太和八年。自浙东观察使又除太子宾客，分司东都，始发州郭。越人父老男女数万，携壶觞至江津相送。</div><div id='poem_preface_27019_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27019'><span -----title
高要
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b61630732c4b44918820668a4e934582_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b61630732c4b44918820668a4e934582");'><span id='b61630732c4b44918820668a4e934582_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=825')">824-825年</a>，53-54岁</div><div id='b61630732c4b44918820668a4e934582' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　秋抵端州，观木槿花有诗。作品：《朱槿花》<div id='poem_26944' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26944' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_26944'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26944'>瘴烟长暖无霜雪，槿艳繁花满树红。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26944_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26944_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=824&endYear=824')">824年</a>　在端州，有诗。作品：《江亭》《红蕉花》《端州亭江得家书二首》《闻猨》《涉沅潇》《逾岭峤止荒陬抵高要》《在端州知家累以九月九日发衡州因寄》<div id='poem_26945' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26945' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26945?labeling=true' target='_blank'>江亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26945")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_26945_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26945'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26945'>瘴江昏雾连天合，欲作家书更断肠。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26945'>今日病身悲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_26945", 26945, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>状候</span>，岂能埋骨向炎荒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26945_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26945'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26945_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27054' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27054' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27054?labeling=true' target='_blank'>红蕉花</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27054")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_27054_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27054'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27054'>红蕉花样炎方识，瘴水溪边色最深。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27054'>叶满丛深殷似火，不唯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27054", 27054, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>烧眼</span>更<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27054", 27054, "Clauses/3/Comments/1")'>烧心</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27054_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27054'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_27054_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26961' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26961' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26961?labeling=true' target='_blank'>端州江亭得家书二首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span /><div class='titleIndent'>七言绝句</div></div><div id='poem_title_26961_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26961'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26961'>雨中鹊语喧江树，风处蛛丝飏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_26961", 26961, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>水浔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26961'>开拆远书何事喜，数行家信抵千金。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26961_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26961'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26961_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26962' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26962' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_26962_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26962'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26962'>长安别日春风早，岭外今来白露秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26962'>莫道淮南悲木叶，不闻摇落更堪愁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26962_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26962'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26962_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_26959' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26959' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_26959'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26959'>见说三声巴峡深，此时行者尽沾襟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26959'>端州江口连云处，始信哀猿伤客心。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26959_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26959'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_26959_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>涉沅潇<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作湘，注内缺二字。）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27066")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27066'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27066'>屈原死处潇湘阴，沧浪淼淼云沈沈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27066'>蛟龙长怒虎长啸，山木翛翛波浪深。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27066'>烟横日落惊鸿起，山映馀<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作云）</span>霞杳<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作淼）</span>千里。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27066'>鸿叫离离入暮天，霞消漠漠深云水。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27066'>水灵<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作虚）</span>江暗扬波涛，鼋鼍动荡风骚骚。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27066'>行人愁望待明月，星汉沈浮𩳤鬼号。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27066'>屈原尔为怀王<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作忠）</span>没，水府通天化灵物。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27066'>何不驱雷击电除奸邪，可怜空作沈泉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>骨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27066'>举杯沥酒招尔魂，月影<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作彩）</span>滉漾开乾坤。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27066'>波白<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作明）</span>水黑山隐见，汨罗之上遥昏昏。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27066'>风帆候晓看五两，戍鼓鼕鼕<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作𪔱𪔱）</span>远山响。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27066'>潮满江津猿鸟啼，荆夫楚语飞蛮桨。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27066'>潇湘岛浦无人居，风惊水暗惟鲛鱼。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27066_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27066'>行来击棹独长叹，问尔精魄何所如。<div id='poem_note_27066'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_7_27066_0'>⑴ 一本此下有抱冤二字</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_27066_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_27071' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27071' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27071?labeling=true' target='_blank'>逾岭峤止荒陬抵高要</a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span "poem_allusion_27071")'>二鲤鱼</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3087, "poem_allusion_27071")'>铜柱</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4696, id='poem_sentence_0_27071'>天将南北分寒燠，北被羔裘南卉服。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27071'>寒气凝为戎虏骄，炎蒸结作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27071", 27071, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>虫虺</span>毒。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27071'>周王止化惟荆蛮，汉武凿远通<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27071", 27071, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>孱颜</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27071'>南标<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(3087, "poem_sentence_3_27071")'>铜柱</span>限荒徼，五岭从兹穷险艰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27071'>衡山截断炎方北，回雁峰南瘴烟黑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27071'>万壑奔伤溢作泷，湍飞浪激如绳直<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27071'>千崖傍耸猿啸悲，丹蛇玄虺潜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_27071", 27071, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>蜲蛇</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27071'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27071", 27071, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>泷夫</span>拟楫劈高浪，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27071", 27071, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>瞥忽</span>浮沈如电随。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27071'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_27071", 27071, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>岭头</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_27071", 27071, "Clauses/16/Comments/1")'>刺竹</span>蒙笼密，火拆红蕉焰烧日。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27071'>岭上泉分南北流，行人照水愁肠骨。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27071'>阴森石路盘萦纡，雨寒日煖常斯须。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27071'>瘴云暂卷火山外，苍茫海气穷番禺。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27071'>鹧鸪猿鸟声相续，椎髻晓呼同戚促。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27071'>百处溪滩异雨晴，四时雷电迷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_27071", 27071, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>昏旭</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27071'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_27071", 27071, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>鱼肠雁足</span>望<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_27071", 27071, "Clauses/28/Comments/1")'>缄封</span>，地远三江岭万重。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27071'>鱼跃岂通清远<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作遂）</span>峡，雁飞难渡漳江东<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_27071'>云蒸地热无霜霰，桃李冬华匪时变。<div id='poem_sentence_16_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_27071'>天际长垂饮涧虹，檐前不去衔泥燕<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_17_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_27071'>幸逢雷雨荡妖昏，提挈悲欢出海门。<div id='poem_sentence_18_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_27071'>西日眼明看少长，北风身醒辨寒温。<div id='poem_sentence_19_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_27071'>贾生谪去因前席，痛哭书成竟何益。<div id='poem_sentence_20_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_27071'>物忌忠良表是非，朝驱<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4696, "poem_sentence_21_27071")'>绛灌</span>为雠敌。<div id='poem_sentence_21_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_27071'>明皇圣德异文皇，不使无辜困鬼方。<div id='poem_sentence_22_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_27071'>汉日<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作口）</span>傅臣终委弃，如今衰叟重辉光。<div id='poem_sentence_23_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_27071'>高明白日恩深海，齿发虽残壮心在。<div id='poem_sentence_24_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_27071'>空愧驽骀异一毛，无令朽骨惭<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作仍）</span>千载。<div id='poem_sentence_25_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_27071'></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_27071_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_27071'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_5_27071_0'>⑴ 南人谓水为泷，如原瀑流，自郴南至韶北，有八泷，其名神泷、伤泷、鸡附等泷，皆急险不可上。南中轻舟迅疾可入此水者，因名之泷船，善游者为泷夫</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_27071_0'>⑵ 余在南中日，知家累以其年九月九日发衡州，因寄云：“菊花开日有人逢，知过衡阳回雁峰。江树送秋黄叶少，海天迎远碧云重。音书断达听蛮鹊，风水多虞祝媪龙。想见病身浑不识，自磨青镜照衰容。”慨然追感，以疏其下。又端州界有清远峡，深险莫测，皆言水府为鱼龙之限也</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_17_27071_0'>⑶ 南中虹四时长见，见数则多飓风，燕不归蛰，燕泥多沙，人惧其沾污于人，每逐其巢也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_27071_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_827393' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_827393' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/827393?labeling=true' target='_blank'>在端州知家累以九月九日发衡州因寄<span class='inlineComment2'>（题拟）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（824年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_827393")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_827393_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_827393'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_827393'>菊花开日有人逢，知过衡阳回雁峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_827393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_827393'>江树送秋黄叶少，海天迎远碧云重。<div id='poem_sentence_1_827393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_827393'>音书断达听蛮鹊，风水多虞祝媪龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_827393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_827393'>想见病身浑不识，自磨青镜照衰容<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_827393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_827393'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_827393_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_827393'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_827393_0'>⑴ 李绅《追昔游诗》卷一《逾岭峤止荒陬抵高要》诗「雁飞难渡漳江东」句下自注引。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_827393_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年2月</a>　携眷游高要县七星岩石室并题名。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=825&endYear=825')">825年4月</a>　大赦天下，李逢吉以李绅之故，于赦书节文内，不言“未量移者，宜与量移”，韦处厚上疏论之，敬宗命追赦书添改。<br /></div>
-----end

-----title
滁州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9ee366c0d4b14d82b9f62ceac7dfd6a8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ee366c0d4b14d82b9f62ceac7dfd6a8");'><span id='9ee366c0d4b14d82b9f62ceac7dfd6a8_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年9月</a>　迁滁州刺史，从江州赴滁州途中有诗。作品：《溯西江》<div id='poem_27043' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27043' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27043?labeling=true' target='_blank'>溯西江</a><span class='authorDate'>（828年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_27043'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27043'>江风不定半晴阴，愁对花时尽日吟。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27043'>孤棹自迟从蹭蹬，乱帆争疾竞<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27043", 27043, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>浮沈</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27043'>一身累困怀千载，百口无虞贵万金。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27043'>空阔远看<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_27043", 27043, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>波浪</span>息，楚山安稳过云岑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27043_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27043'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27043_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年9月</a>　迁滁州刺史，从江州赴滁州早发有诗。作品：《早发》<div id='poem_26979' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26979' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_26979'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26979'>沙洲月落<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_26979", 26979, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>宿禽</span>惊，潮起风微晓雾生。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26979'>黄鹤浪明知上信，黑龙山暗避前程。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26979'>火旗似辨吴门戍，水驿遥迷楚塞城。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26979'>萧索更看江叶下，两乡俱是宦游情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26979_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26979'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26979_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=828&endYear=828')">828年</a>　在滁州任，于西园广植桃李，常游滁州琅琊山。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在滁州任。作品：《追和韦应物《登北楼》（残句）》《东园（今佚）》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=829&endYear=829')">829年</a>　在滁州任，有客善弹琵琶，乃善才所授，时善才已没，赋诗追感往事。作品：《悲善才》<div id='poem_27069' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27069' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27069?labeling=true' target='_blank'>悲善才</a><span class='authorDate'>（829年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27069")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27069_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27069'>余守郡日，有客游者，善弹琵琶，问其所传，乃善才所授。顷在内庭日，别承恩顾，赐宴曲江，敕善才等二十人备乐。自余经播迁，善才已没。因追感前事，为悲善才。</div><div id='poem_preface_27069_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27069'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27069'>穆王夜幸蓬池曲，金銮殿开高秉烛。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27069'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27069", 27069, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>东头</span>弟子曹善才，琵琶请进<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作奏）</span>新翻曲。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27069'>翠蛾列坐层城女，笙笛<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作歌）</span>参差齐笑语。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27069'>天颜静听朱丝弹，众乐寂然无敢举。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27069'>衔花金凤当承拨，转腕拢<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作笼）</span>弦促<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_27069", 27069, "Clauses/9/Comments/2")'>挥抹</span><span id='poem_sentence_5_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27069'>抽弦度曲新声发，金铃玉佩相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_27069", 27069, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>瑳切</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27069'>流莺子母飞上林，仙鹤雌雄唳明月。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27069'>此时奉诏侍金銮，别殿承恩许召弹<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作看）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27069'>三月曲江春草绿，九霄天乐下云端。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27069'>紫髯供奉前屈膝，尽弹妙曲当春日。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27069'>寒泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_27069", 27069, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>注射</span>陇水开，胡雁翻飞向<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作朔）</span>天没。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27069'>日曛尘暗车马散，为惜新声有馀叹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27069'>明年冠剑闭桥山，万里孤臣投海畔。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27069'>笼<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作离）</span>禽铩翮<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作羽）</span>尚还<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作强回）</span>飞，白首生从五岭归。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27069'>闻道善才成<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_27069", 27069, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>朽骨</span>，空馀弟子奉音<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作宣）</span>徽。<div id='poem_sentence_15_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_27069'>南谯寂寞三春晚，有客弹弦独<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_27069", 27069, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>凄怨</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_16_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_27069'>静听深奏楚月光，忆昔初闻曲江宴。<div id='poem_sentence_17_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_27069'>心悲不觉泪阑干，更为调弦反覆弹。<div id='poem_sentence_18_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_27069'>秋吹动摇神女佩，月珠<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_27069", 27069, id='poem_sentence_20_27069_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_27069'>惆怅追怀万事空，雍门感慨<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作琴瑟）</span>徒为尔。<div 寿县

href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=830&endYear=830')">830年2月</a>　转寿州刺史，离滁州时，乡人留恋，绅有诗记之。作品：《闻里谣效古歌》<div id='poem_27065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>闻里谣效古歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（830年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a id='poem_sentence_1_27065'>兄锄弟耨妻在机，夜犬不吠开蓬扉。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27065'>乡里儿，醉还饱，浊醪初熟劝翁媪<span id='poem_sentence_3_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27065'>劝年少，乐耕桑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27065'>父渔子猎日归暮<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作父子猎归白日暮）</span>，月明处处舂黄粱。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27065'>莫令太守驰朱轓，悬鼓一鸣<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_27065", 27065, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>卢鹊</span>喧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27065'>恶声主吏噪尔门，唧唧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_27065", 27065, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>力力</span>烹鸡豚。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27065'>乡里儿，莫悲咤。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27065'>上有明王颁诏下，重选贤良恤孤寡。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27065'>春日迟迟驱五马，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_27065", 27065, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>留犊</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_27065", 27065, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>投钱</span>以为谢。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27065_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=831&endYear=831')">831年</a>　在寿州任，郁浑应百篇举，李绅命百题试之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　在寿州任，荐郁浑应百篇科。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　在寿州任，作品：《寿州法华院石经堂记》<div id='poem_1373681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寿州法华院石经堂记</a><span class='authorDate'>（832年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373681")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373681'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373681'>如来以万门万行。普示群生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373681_comment'></div>随其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1373681", 1373681, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>性根</span>。用假方便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373681_comment'></div>水月观象。万泉俱鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373681_comment'></div>识真如者。知非在水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373681_comment'></div>慧灯传照。百千同朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373681_comment'></div>识佛智者。知灯在觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373681_comment'></div>是以如来开三乘谕。演菩提旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373681_comment'></div>传十二轮。度生死海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373681_comment'></div>是经之要妙。诸佛之心印。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373681_comment'></div>卷舒万法。彰示凡圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373681_comment'></div>信解得入。入为真谛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373681_comment'></div>无我无我。无为无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373681_comment'></div>无生无生。无灭无灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373681_comment'></div>诸佛如来。不以寂灭自乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373681_comment'></div>无生自处。故现生灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373681_comment'></div>以示群迷。入烦恼中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373681_comment'></div>解众生縳。入有相中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373681_comment'></div>示众生灭。是以诸佛如来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373681_comment'></div>以一切众生烦恼苦海无明罪垢为解脱方便。故经有火宅穷子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373681_comment'></div>以宏法谕。有众生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373681_comment'></div>有烦恼。离烦恼即诸佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373681_comment'></div>有烦恼即众生。烦恼盖缠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373681_comment'></div>不知明觉。如寐如病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373681_comment'></div>佛为解寐疗病。众生昏业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373681_comment'></div>不能解释。故如来广清净教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373681_comment'></div>开是经典。用晓迷愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373681_comment'></div>以示方便。闻是经者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373681_comment'></div>发菩提心。持是经者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1373681_comment'></div>入如来智。一礼一敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1373681_comment'></div>皆资胜因。刻于贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1373681_comment'></div>瞻仰常睹。表佛慈旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1373681_comment'></div>无言现言。刊诸莲宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1373681_comment'></div>永乘福慧。太和六年岁在壬子七月既望缺之二日书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1373681_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1373681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=832&endYear=832')">832年</a>　在寿州任，寿州盛唐县有连理二株，绅亲临考察视为瑞物，十二月罢寿州刺史时，绅有诗，并将瑞物写入诗篇。作品：《寿阳罢郡日有诗十首与追怀不殊今编于后兼纪瑞物》<div id='poem_26999' class='_poem'><div
