ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年2月</a>　赴洛阳途经濠州，游四望亭，有记。作品：《四望亭记》<div id='poem_1373682' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1373682' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1373682?labeling=true' target='_blank'>四望亭记</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_1373682")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1373682_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1373682'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1373682'>濠城之西北隅。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1373682", 1373682, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>爽耸</span>四达。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1373682_comment'></div>纵目周视。回环者可数百里而远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1373682_comment'></div>尽彼目力。四封不阅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1373682_comment'></div>尝为废墉。无所伫望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1373682_comment'></div>郡守彭城刘君字嗣之理郡之二载。步履所及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1373682_comment'></div>悦而创亭焉。丰约广袤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1373682_comment'></div>称其所便。栋干<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1373682", 1373682, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>梯陛</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1373682_comment'></div>依墉以成。崇不危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1373682_comment'></div>丽不侈。可以列宾筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1373682_comment'></div>可以施管磬。云山左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1373682_comment'></div>长淮萦带。下绕清濠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1373682_comment'></div>旁阚城邑。四封五通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1373682_comment'></div>皆可洞然。太和七年春二月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1373682_comment'></div>绅分命东洛。路出于濠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1373682_comment'></div>始登斯亭。周目四瞩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1373682_comment'></div>美乎哉。春台视和气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1373682_comment'></div>夏日居高明。秋以阅农功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1373682_comment'></div>冬以观肃成。盖君子布和求瘼之诚志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1373682_comment'></div>岂徒纵目于白雪。望云于黄鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1373682_comment'></div>庾楼夕月。岘首春风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1373682_comment'></div>盖一时之胜爽。无四者之眺临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1373682_comment'></div>斯亭之佳景。固难俦俪哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1373682_comment'></div>淮柳初变。濠泉始清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1373682_comment'></div>山凝远岚。霞散馀绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1373682_comment'></div>顾余尝为玉堂词臣。笔砚犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1373682_comment'></div>请书亭表事。刻石记言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1373682_comment'></div>癸丑岁建卯月七日。赵郡李绅书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1373682_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1373682_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
洛阳

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年4月6日</a>　除河南尹，有诗纪之。作品：《拜三川守》<div id='poem_27008' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27008' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27008?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜三川守</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年4月6日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27008")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27008_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27008'>开成元年三月二十五日，蒙恩除河南尹。四月六日，诏下洛阳。是月自春不雨，已踰六旬。此日谢恩，未诣公府，驰祷龙祠。止九日，大降膏泽，连霪浃日，时苗顿茂。又里巷比多恶少，皆免帽散衣（皆危帽散衣），聚为群斗，或差肩追绕击大毬，里言谓之打棍谙论。士庶苦之，车马逢者不敢前，都城为患日久。诏下之日，此辈皆失所在，欲归负贩之业，闾里间无复前患。</div><div id='poem_preface_27008_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27008'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(781, "poem_allusion_27008")'>辨鲁鱼</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1224, "poem_allusion_27008")'>偃草</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8090, "poem_allusion_27008")'>随车</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27008_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27008'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27008'>恭承宠诏临伊洛，静守朝章化比闾。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27008'>风变市儿惊<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1224, "poem_sentence_1_27008")'>偃草</span>，雨晴郊薮谬<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8090, "poem_sentence_1_27008")'>随车</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27008'>改张琴瑟移<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27008", 27008, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>胶柱</span>，止息<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27008", 27008, "Clauses/5/Comments/1")'>笙篁</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(781, "poem_sentence_2_27008")'>辨鲁鱼</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27008_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27008'>唯有从容期一德，使齐文教奉皇居。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年5月</a>　任河南尹，白居易自编文集并撰记，李绅题诗附于记后。作品：《看题文集后记因成四韵以美之（或作题白乐天文集）》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年6月</a>　任河南尹，祭中岳，宿少林寺，有题少林寺诗。作品：《庆云见》《灵蛇见少林寺》<div id='poem_26978' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26978' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26978?labeling=true' target='_blank'>庆云见</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26978")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26978_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_26978'>夏六月，准诏祭中岳，宿少林寺，祭毕归寺。有庆云见于峰，初如绛绡蒙覆上下，岩树透彻，虚明照日。俄顷，诸崖谷间尽祥云，纷郁绵布，自午至未不散。</div><div id='poem_preface_26978_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26978'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26978'>礼成中岳陈金册，祥报卿云冠玉峰。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26978'>轻未透林疑待凤，细非行雨讵从龙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26978'>还入九霄成沆瀣，夕岚生处鹤归松。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26978_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26978'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26978_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_27001' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27001' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27001?labeling=true' target='_blank'>灵蛇见少林寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27001")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27001_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27001'>二大松上有青蛇，不知所自。下马之际，忽坠于地，盘结异状，若紫组绶。青光荧射，逼之不怒。问其寺僧，僧云：「尝见。」因令祝以箱奁引之，遂逶迤就器。送寺外，倏忽如失之。</div><div id='poem_preface_27001_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27001'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27001'>琐文结绶灵蛇降，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27001", 27001, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>蠖屈螭盘</span>顾视闲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27001'>鳞蹙翠光抽璀璨，腹连金彩动弯环。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27001'>已应<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27001", 27001, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>蜕骨</span>风雷后，岂效衔珠草莽间。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27001'>知尔全身护昆阆，不矜挥尾在常山。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27001_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27001'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27001_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: href='/Writing/27009?labeling=true' target='_blank'>拜宣武军节度使</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年7月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_27009'>开成元年六月二十六日，制授宣武军节度使。七月三日，中使刘泰押送旌节止洛阳，五日赴镇。出都门，城内少长士女相送者数万人，至白马寺，涕泣当车者不可止。少尹严元容鞭胥吏市人，怒其恋慕，留台御史杜牧使台吏遮欧百姓，令其废祖帐。</div><div id='poem_preface_27009_comment'></div><div 宜昌

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=833&endYear=833')">833年</a>　渡西陵，作诗，姑系于此。作品：《渡西陵十六韵》<div id='poem_27050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>渡西陵十六韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（833年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27050")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27050_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27050'>七年冬，十有三日，早渡浙江，寒雨方霖，军吏悉在江次。越人年谷未成，霪雨不止，田亩浸溢，水不及穗者数寸。余至驿，命押衙裴行宗先赍祝辞，东望拜大禹庙，且以百姓请命，雨收云息，日朗者三旬有五日，刈穫皆毕，有以见神之不欺也。</div><div id='poem_preface_27050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27050'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27050'>雨送奔涛远，风收骇浪平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27050'>截流张旆影，分岸走鼙声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27050'>兽逐衔波涌，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27050", 27050, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>龟艨</span>喷棹轻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27050'>海门凝雾暗，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_27050", 27050, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>江渚</span>湿云横。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27050'>雁翼看舟子，鱼鳞辨水营。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27050'>骑交遮戍合，戈簇拥沙明。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27050'>谬履千夫长，将询百吏情。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27050'>下车占黍稷，冬雨害粢盛。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27050'>望祷依前圣，垂休翼厚生。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27050'>半江犹惨澹，全野已澄清。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27050'>爱景三辰朗，祥农万庾盈。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27050'>浦程通曲屿，海色媚重城。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27050'>弓日<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_27050", 27050, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>鞬櫜</span>动，旗风虎豹争。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_preface_26991'>出杭州界入苏州，八年。浙西六郡灾旱，百姓饥殍，道路相望，米价翔贵，是岁。浙东大稔，因请出米五万斛贱估，以救浙西居人，诏下蒙允。是岁，王璠不奏饥旱，反怒邻境所救，以为卖己，遂与王涯合计诬搆。罔上奏陈，米非官米，足私求利，及璠伏诛，蒙圣恩加察奸邪所罔。初入浙西苏州界，吴人以恤灾之惠，犹惧旌幡留戒于迥野之处，不及城郭之所，则相率拜泣于舟楫前。是岁，卢周仁为苏州刺史。</div><div id='poem_preface_26991_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_26991'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4754, id='poem_sentence_0_27044'>香灯寂莫网尘中，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27044", 27044, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>烦恼身</span>须色界空。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27044'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27044", 27044, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>龙钵</span>已倾无法雨，虎床犹在有悲风。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27044'>定心池上浮泡没，招手岩边梦幻通。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27044'>深夜月明松子落，俨然听法侍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_27044", 27044, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>生公</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27044_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27044'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27044_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴任洛阳途中，毗陵东山，有诗，姑系于此。作品：《毗陵东山》<div id='poem_27010' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27010' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27010?labeling=true' target='_blank'>毗陵东山</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27010")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27010_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27010'>东山在毗陵驿，南连水西馆，馆即独孤及在郡所置，荒废已久。至孟公简重修，植以花木松竹等，可玩。孟公在郡日，余以校书郎从役，同宴于此，今则荒废仍旧。</div><div id='poem_preface_27010_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27010'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27010'>昔人别馆淹留处，卜筑东山学谢家。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27010'>业桂半空摧枳棘，曲池平尽隔烟霞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27010'>重开渔浦连天月<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作日）</span>，更种春园满地花。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27010'>依旧秋风还寂莫，数行衰柳宿啼鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27010'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27010_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_27010'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(27010)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴任洛阳途中，有诗，姑系于此。作品：《建元寺》<div id='poem_27003' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27003' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27003?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建元寺<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作和郭郧寒食）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27003")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_27003_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27003'>寺在常州东郭（常州建元寺，在郡东郭），松扉竹院，各在冈阜，地甚疏通，连接郊外每岁寒食里人洒扫经过之所。大历中，诗人郭云（郭郧）曾赋寒食诗赠吏部先兄。诗云：「兰陵士女满晴川，郊外纷纷拜古埏。万井人家初禁火，九原松柏自生烟。人间后事非前事，镜里今年老去年。介子终知禄不及，王孙谁复更相怜。」当时以为绝唱，尝在童儿，即闻此诗，非欲继和，盖纪事因书。</div><div id='poem_preface_27003_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27003'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27003'>江城物候伤心地，远寺经过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_27003", 27003, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>禁火辰</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27003'>芳草垄边回首客，野花丛里断肠人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27003'>紫荆繁艳空门昼，红药深开古殿春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27003'>叹息光阴催白发，莫悲风月独沾巾。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27003_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27003'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27003_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴任洛阳途中，宿瓜州，有诗。作品：《宿瓜州》<div id='poem_27016' id='poem_sentence_3_27016'>官冷旧谙唯旅馆，岁阴轻薄是凉飙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27016_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27016'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27016_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>赴任洛阳途中，入扬州，有诗。作品：《入扬州郭》<div id='poem_26964' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26964' href='/Writing/27012?labeling=true' target='_blank'>重别西湖</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_preface_27012'>东去日前，别湖中双鸂鶒（别西湖双鸂鶒）、翡翠、早梅等三题。及西来，则鸂鶒、翡翠悉皆翔失，梅衰秋叶，重起前叹耳。</div><div id='poem_preface_27012_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27012'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27012'>浦边梅叶看凋落，波上双禽去寂寥。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27012'>吹管曲传花易失，织文机学羽难飘。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27012'>雪欺春早摧芳萼，隼励<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27012", 27012, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>秋深</span>拂翠翘。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27012'>繁艳彩毛无处所，尽成愁叹别溪桥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27012_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27012'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_27012_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

-----title
泗县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e52366d7432d4aff93de184d866c31f4_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e52366d7432d4aff93de184d866c31f4");'><span id='e52366d7432d4aff93de184d866c31f4_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>，64岁</div><div id='e52366d7432d4aff93de184d866c31f4' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=835&endYear=835')">835年</a>　赴任洛阳途中，入泗口，有诗。作品：《却入泗口》<div id='poem_26988' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_26988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/26988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>却入泗口</a><span class='authorDate'>（835年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_26988")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_26988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_26988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_26988'>洪河一派清淮接，堤草芦花万里秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_26988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_26988'>烟树寂寥<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作苍茫）</span>分楚泽，海云明灭满<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作见）</span>扬州。<div id='poem_sentence_1_26988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_26988'>望深江汉连天远，思起乡闾<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作关）</span>满眼愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_26988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_26988'>惆怅路岐真<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作惟）</span>此处，夕阳西没水东流。<div id='poem_sentence_3_26988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_26988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_26988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_26988'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(26988)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
开封
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='92d673f2fb9848c484931772294fad96_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("92d673f2fb9848c484931772294fad96");'><span id='92d673f2fb9848c484931772294fad96_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年7月12日</a>　到汴州任，有诗纪之。作品：《到宣武三十韵》<div id='poem_27049' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27049' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27049?labeling=true' target='_blank'>到宣武三十韵</a><span class='authorDate'>（836年7月12日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27049")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_27049_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_preface_27049'>七月十二日到汴州。是月，郑汴间不雨已馀月，秋苗已悴。十日至圃田，天雨已馀。至十二日朝旨，秋稼顿茂，军礼亦成矣。</div><div id='poem_preface_27049_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27049'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2790, "poem_allusion_27049")'>客卿</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6785, "poem_allusion_27049")'>卫青</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(8734, "poem_allusion_27049")'>信陵</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9939, "poem_allusion_27049")'>义夫</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27049_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27049'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27049'>七月趋梁苑，三年谢尹京。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27049'>旧风除物蠹，新律奉师贞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27049'>龙节双油重，蛇矛百练明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27049'>跃鱼连后旆，腾虎耀前旌。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27049'>路转金神并，川开铁马横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27049'>拥旄差白羽，分辔引红缨。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27049'>在浚风烟接，维嵩巩洛清。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27049'>贯鱼奔骑疾，连雁卷行轻。<div "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>烟垒</span>风调角，秋原雨洗兵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27049'>宿云看<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_27049", 27049, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>布甲</span>，疏柳见分营。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27049'>鼓彻通宵警，和门候晓晴。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27049'>虎符三校列，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_27049", 27049, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>鱼胄</span>万夫迎。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27049'>弄马猿猱健，奔车角抵呈。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27049'>驾肩傍隘道，张幕内连楹。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27049'>森戟承三令，攒戈退一声。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_27049'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9939, "poem_sentence_17_27049")'>义夫</span>留感激，公子播英名。<div id='poem_sentence_17_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_27049'>泽广豚鱼洽，恩宣岂弟生。<div id='poem_sentence_18_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_27049'>善师忘任智，中略在推诚。<div id='poem_sentence_19_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_27049'>式宴歌钟合，陈筵绮绣并。<div id='poem_sentence_20_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_27049'>戏鼙千卒跃，均酒百壶倾。<div id='poem_sentence_21_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_27049'>乐与师徒共，欢从井邑盈。<div id='poem_sentence_22_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_27049'>教通因渐染，人悦尚和平。<div id='poem_sentence_23_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_27049'>授钺惭分阃，登坛荷列城。<div id='poem_sentence_24_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_27049'>虚裘朝独坐，雄剑夜孤鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_25_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_27049'>白发侵霜变，丹心捧日惊。<div onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6785, "poem_sentence_28_27049")'>期月</span>终迷化，三年讵有成。<div id='poem_sentence_28_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_27049'>惟看波海动，天外斩长鲸。<div id='poem_sentence_29_27049_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_27049'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_27049_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=836&endYear=836')">836年</a>　在汴州任。作品：《移九江》<div id='poem_27068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/27068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>移九江<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup></a><span class='authorDate'>（836年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(16981, "唐", "李绅", "poem_title_27068")'>李绅</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_27068_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_27068_0'>① 效何水部，余自九江及今，周一纪矣。</div></div></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_27068'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(284, "poem_allusion_27068")'>白驹催</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(340, "poem_allusion_27068")'>俗眼白</span>　<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9502, "poem_allusion_27068")'>悬磬</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_27068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_27068'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_27068'>秋波入白水，帆去侵空小。<div id='poem_sentence_0_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_27068'>五两剧奔星，樯乌疾飞鸟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27068'>盆城依落日，盆浦看云眇。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27068'>云眇更苍苍，匡山低夕阳。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_27068'>楚客喜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_27068", 27068, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>风水</span>，秦人悲异乡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_27068'>异乡秋思苦，江皋月华吐。<div id='poem_sentence_5_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_27068'>漾漾隐波亭，悠悠通月浦。<div id='poem_sentence_6_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_27068'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_27068", 27068, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>津桥</span>归候吏，竹巷开门户。<div id='poem_sentence_7_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_27068'>容膝有匡床，及肩才数堵。<div id='poem_sentence_8_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_27068'>隙光非白驹，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9502, "poem_sentence_9_27068")'>悬磬</span>我无虞。<div id='poem_sentence_9_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_27068'>体瘦寡行立，家肥安<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_27068", 27068, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>啜哺</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_10_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_27068'>天书怜谴谪，重作朱轓客。<div id='poem_sentence_11_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_27068'>四座眼全青，一麾头半白。<div id='poem_sentence_12_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_27068'>今来思往事，往事益悽然。<div id='poem_sentence_13_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_27068'>风月同今昔，悲欢异目前。<div id='poem_sentence_14_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_27068'>四时嗟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_27068", 27068, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>阅水</span>，一纪换流年。<div id='poem_sentence_15_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_27068'>独有西庭鹤，孤鸣白露天。<div id='poem_sentence_16_27068_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_27068'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_27068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　在汴州任，奏“蝗虫入境，不食田苗”<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　在汴州任，于汴州置利润楼店。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=837&endYear=837')">837年</a>　在汴州任，有诗酬白居易《立秋夕有怀》作品：《奉酬乐天立秋夕有怀见寄》<div id='poem_27062' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_27062' class='poemTitle onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_27062", 27062, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>阶篁</span>淅沥响，露叶参差光。<div id='poem_sentence_1_27062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_27062'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_27062", 27062, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>冰兔</span>半升魄，铜壶微滴<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作漏）</span>长。<div id='poem_sentence_2_27062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_27062'>薄帷乍飘卷，襟带轻摇飏。<div id='poem_sentence_3_27062_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
